\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Universal Asynchronous Receiver/\+Transmitter (\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}}) driver for X\+MC microcontroller family. 

The \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} driver uses Universal Serial Interface Channel(\+U\+S\+I\+C) module to implement \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} protocol. It provides A\+P\+Is to configure U\+S\+IC channel for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication. The driver enables the user in getting the status of \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} protocol events, configuring interrupt service requests, protocol related parameter configuration etc.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} driver features\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Configuration structure X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+t and initialization function \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ga719ad21f9ccaf9585dd0b473b4daef7e}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Init()}}
\item Enumeration of events with their bit masks \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ga22c103e1b9722a590bbe623c51748667}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_gab1d2c007983f53c2965757f021c5fa69}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+t}}
\item Allows the selection of input source for the D\+X0 input stage using the A\+PI \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_gae5f466fb1df22b9039936ed4e39f527a}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Input\+Source()}}
\item Allows configuration of baudrate using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ga0f757d62a86fc8944cf7188137490b62}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Baudrate()}} and configuration of data length using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_gab6f5a7ef41affa10c0190b50d90b2f68}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Word\+Length()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ga2c9c799602a222b33bdca80aab23e073}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Length()}}
\item Provides the status of \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} protocol events, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_gaf6374dc527b7a69200f266c715badec8}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Get\+Status\+Flag()}}
\item Allows transmission of data using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ga3a9b41f5d74a0dde43d9b19166ffa7c6}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Transmit()}} and gets received data using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ga578c15fc0df2e8ea7a265c92c0a26536}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Get\+Received\+Data()}} 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

{\em flag} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} events to be cleared. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} Use \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_gab1d2c007983f53c2965757f021c5fa69}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+t}} enumerations for event bitmasks. \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ggaf673b8181ec8cd10bc19d476716aaddfa8838558f1c949dfdfa117908e21d7058}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+M\+I\+S\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+I\+D\+LE}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ggaf673b8181ec8cd10bc19d476716aaddfa02d60fc761d9eee4c4d1c525f2429a5c}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+E\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+I\+D\+LE}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ggaf673b8181ec8cd10bc19d476716aaddfaeaf9ee65696e36e06e012e0e3e5b5855}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+N\+C\+H\+R\+O\+N\+I\+Z\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+B\+R\+E\+A\+K\+\_\+\+D\+E\+T\+E\+C\+T\+ED}} etc. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Clears the status of \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} channel events.~\newline
~\newline
Multiple events can be combined using the bitwise OR operation and configured in one function call. X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+t enumerates multiple event bitmasks. These enumerations can be used as input to the A\+PI. Events are cleared by setting the bitmask to the P\+S\+CR register.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Disables the interrupt events by clearing the bits in C\+CR register.~\newline
~\newline
Multiple events can be combined using the bitwise OR operation and configured in one function call. X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+t enumerates multiple event bitmasks. These enumerations can be used as input to the A\+PI.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Enable data transmission.~\newline
~\newline
Use this function in combination with \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_gacf473597e714fcc6f41e45d0a5d7f99c}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Disable\+Data\+Transmission()}} to fill the F\+I\+FO and send the F\+I\+FO content without gaps in the transmission. F\+I\+FO is filled using \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gacc0a4521925fd852e7e08075235d85fb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+T\+X\+F\+I\+F\+O\+\_\+\+Put\+Data()}}. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you need more control over the start of transmission use \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_ga04c66a47ae22c847b394f10d85e01bf8}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Start\+Transmision\+Mode()}}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Enables interrupt events for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication.~\newline
~\newline
Multiple events can be combined using the bitwise OR operation and configured in one function call. \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ga22c103e1b9722a590bbe623c51748667}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+t}} enumerates multiple event bitmasks. These enumerations can be used as input to the A\+PI. Events are configured by setting bits in the C\+CR register. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint16\+\_\+t Received data over \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication channel. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Provides one word of data received over \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication channel.~\newline
~\newline
Based on the channel configuration, data is either read from the receive F\+I\+FO or R\+B\+UF register. Before returning the value, there is no check for data validity. User should check the appropriate data receive flags(standard receive/alternative receive/\+F\+I\+FO standard receive/\+F\+I\+FO alternative receive) before executing the A\+PI. Reading from an empty receive F\+I\+FO can generate a receive error event.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Provides the status of \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} channel events.~\newline
~\newline
Status provided by the A\+PI represents the status of multiple events at their bit positions. The bitmasks can be obtained using the enumeration X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+t. Event status is obtained by reading the register P\+S\+R\+\_\+\+A\+S\+C\+Mode.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+t Status of initializing the U\+S\+IC channel for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} protocol.~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ggae2a1514ed1a18d0d8ba09815dbb3201ba1d4d4ea36dc6c0ceb6599efed42f0559}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+OK}} if initialization is successful.~\newline
 \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ggae2a1514ed1a18d0d8ba09815dbb3201ba146ec14a2e6f316f449c332a863289b0}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR}} if configuration of baudrate failed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Initializes the U\+S\+IC channel for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} protocol.~\newline
~\newline
During the initialization, U\+S\+IC channel is enabled, baudrate is configured with the defined oversampling value in the intialization structure. If the oversampling value is set to 0 in the structure, the default oversampling of 16 is considered. Sampling point for each symbol is configured at the half of sampling period. Symbol value is decided by the majority decision among 3 samples. Word length is configured with the number of data bits. If the value of {\itshape frame\+\_\+length} is 0, then U\+S\+IC channel frame length is set to the same value as word length. If {\itshape frame\+\_\+length} is greater than 0, it is set as the U\+S\+IC channel frame length. Parity mode is set to the value configured for {\itshape parity\+\_\+mode}. The U\+S\+IC channel should be set to \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} mode by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ga65b28640516b5abd6946861b8e069dc5}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Start()}} A\+PI after the initialization.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Sets the interrupt node for U\+S\+IC channel events. ~\newline
~\newline
For an event to generate interrupt, node pointer should be configured with service request(S\+R0, S\+R1..S\+R5). The N\+V\+IC node gets linked to the interrupt event by doing so.~\newline
 Note\+: N\+V\+IC node should be separately enabled to generate the interrupt.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & Constant pointer to U\+S\+IC channel handle of type \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} ~\newline

Availability of U\+A\+R\+T1 and U\+A\+R\+T2 depends on device selection 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em rate} & Desired baudrate. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} minimum value = 100, maximum value depends on the peripheral clock frequency~\newline
 and {\itshape oversampling}. Maximum baudrate can be derived using the formula\+: (fperiph $\ast$ 1023)/(1024 $\ast$ oversampling) \\
\hline
{\em oversampling} & Required oversampling. The value indicates the number of time quanta for one symbol of data.~\newline
 This can be related to the number of samples for each logic state of the data signal.~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} 4 to 32. Value should be chosen based on the protocol used. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+t Status indicating the baudrate configuration.~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_ggac2093935c82fd30f2de4c135d00fb201a7f5eeda6309c7b3a3e8f08380ed47e3c}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+OK}} if baudrate is successfully configured, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_ggac2093935c82fd30f2de4c135d00fb201af9cf48d10eb977902d20eeaed491bcf0}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR}} if desired baudrate or oversampling is invalid.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Sets the bus speed in bits per second.~\newline
~\newline
Derives the values of {\itshape S\+T\+EP} and P\+D\+IV to arrive at the optimum realistic speed possible. {\itshape oversampling} is the number of samples to be taken for each symbol of \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} protocol. Default {\itshape oversampling} of 16 is considered if the input {\itshape oversampling} is less than 4. It is recommended to keep a minimum oversampling of 4 for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}}.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

{\em frame\+\_\+length} & Number of data bits in each \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} frame. ~\newline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Sets the number of data bits for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication.~\newline
~\newline
The frame length is configured by setting the input value to {\itshape S\+C\+TR} register. The value of {\itshape frame\+\_\+length} will be decremented by 1, before setting it to the register. Frame length should not be set to 64 for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

Sets input soource for the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication.~\newline

Sets the interrupt node for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} channel protocol events.~\newline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+Set\+Word\+Length (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{channel,  }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t}]{word\+\_\+length }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & Constant pointer to U\+S\+IC channel handle of type \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} ~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T0\+\_\+\+C\+H0, X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T0\+\_\+\+C\+H1,X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T1\+\_\+\+C\+H0,X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T1\+\_\+\+C\+H1,X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T2\+\_\+\+C\+H0,X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T2\+\_\+\+C\+H1 \\

\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Availability of U\+A\+R\+T1 and U\+A\+R\+T2 depends on device selection 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em word\+\_\+length} & Data word length. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} minimum= 1, maximum= 16. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Sets the data word length in number of bits.~\newline
~\newline
Word length can range from 1 to 16. It indicates the number of data bits in a data word. The value of {\itshape word\+\_\+length} will be decremented by 1 before setting the value to {\itshape S\+C\+TR} register. If the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} data bits is more than 16, then the frame length should be set to the actual number of bits and word length should be configured with the number of bits expected in each transaction. For example, if number of data bits for \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication is 20 bits, then the frame length should be set as 20. Word length can be set based on the transmit and receive handling. If data is stored as 8bit array, then the word length can be set to 8. In this case, a full message of \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} data should be transmitted/ received as 3 data words.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}

~\newline
~\newline

\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel} & Constant pointer to U\+S\+IC channel handle of type \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_s_i_c_gab79a19dac84ff17c48b06cfa3b38ecc3}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+t}} ~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T0\+\_\+\+C\+H0, X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T0\+\_\+\+C\+H1,X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T1\+\_\+\+C\+H0,X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T1\+\_\+\+C\+H1,X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T2\+\_\+\+C\+H0,X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T2\+\_\+\+C\+H1 \\

\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Sets the U\+S\+IC channel operation mode to \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} mode.~\newline
~\newline
C\+CR register bitfield {\itshape Mode} is set to 2(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} mode). This A\+PI should be called after configuring the U\+S\+IC channel. Transmission and reception can happen only when the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} mode is set. This is an inline function.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

 \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ggae2a1514ed1a18d0d8ba09815dbb3201ba1d4d4ea36dc6c0ceb6599efed42f0559}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+OK}} if the communication channel is stopped. \mbox{\hyperlink{group___u_a_r_t_ggae2a1514ed1a18d0d8ba09815dbb3201ba410817c31e098fd03c04f4d5ecb76ef1}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+U\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+B\+U\+SY}} if the communication channel is busy.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Stops the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} communication.~\newline
~\newline
C\+CR register bitfield {\itshape Mode} is reset. This disables the communication. Before starting the communication again, the channel has to be reconfigured.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em data} & Data to be transmitted. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{Range\+:}} 16 bit unsigned data within the range 0 to 65535. Actual size of data transmitted depends on the configured number of bits for the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} protocol in the register S\+C\+TR. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description}
Transmits data over serial communication channel using \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_u_a_r_t}{U\+A\+RT}} protocol.~\newline
~\newline
Based on the channel configuration, data is either put to the transmit F\+I\+FO or to T\+B\+UF register. Before putting data to T\+B\+UF, the A\+PI waits for T\+B\+UF to finish shifting its contents to shift register. So user can continuously execute the A\+PI without checking for T\+B\+UF busy status. Based on the number of data bits configured, the lower significant bits will be extracted for transmission.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
Note\+: When F\+I\+FO is not configured, the A\+PI waits for the T\+B\+UF to be available. This makes the execution a blocking call.

~\newline
~\newline

\end{DoxyParagraph}
